CrashId = store_crash(Error, Stacktrace, Analysis),\\n    {reply, {CrashId, Analysis}, State};\\n\\nhandle_call({auto_fix, CrashId}, _From, State) ->\\n    case ets:lookup(?CRASH_TABLE, CrashId) of\\n ets:delete_all_objects(?CRASH_TABLE),\\n    {reply, ok, State};\\n\\nhandle_call(_Req, _From, State) ->\\n    {reply, {error, unknown}, State}.\\n\\nhandle_cast(_Msg, State) ->\\n    {noreply, end,\\n    {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info({'DOWN', Ref, process, Pid, Reason}, State = #state{monitored = Monitored}) ->\\n    % A monitored process crashed\\n    case maps:get(Pid, Monitored, erlang:system_time(millisecond)\\n            },\\n            CrashId = store_crash(crash, Reason, CrashInfo),\\n            io:format(\\\"[healer] Process ~p (~p) crashed: ~p~n\\\", [Pid, Module, true ->\\n                    case Reason of\\n                        normal -> ok;  % Normal exit, don't heal\\n                        _ -> \\n                            io:format(\\\"[healer] timer:send_after(1000, {remonitor, Module})\\n                    end;\\n                false -> ok\\n            end,\\n            {noreply, State#state{monitored = NewMonitored}};\\n        undefined ->\\n            % Unknown process\\n            {noreply, State}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_info({remonitor, Module}, State = #state{monitored = Monitored}) ->\\n    % Try to re-monitor a              undefined ->\\n                    Ref = monitor(process, Pid),\\n                    NewMonitored = Monitored#{Pid => {Module, Ref}},\\n                    io:format(\\\"[healer] Re-monitored ~p (pid ~p)~n\\\", [Module, Pid]),\\n                    {noreply, State#state{monitored = NewMonitored}};\\n                _ ->\\n                    {noreply, State}\\n            end\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_info({'EXIT', Pid, Reason}, State) ->\\n    Stacktrace = try throw(capture) catch throw:capture:St -> St end,\\n    CrashInfo = #{\\n        type => exit,\\n        pid => State}.\\n\\nterminate(_Reason, _State) ->\\n    ok.\\n\\ncode_change(_OldVsn, State, _Extra) ->\\n    {ok, State}.\\n\\nanalyze_crash(Error, Stacktrace) ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, {analyze_crash, Error, Stacktrace}).\\n\\nauto_fix(CrashId) ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, {auto_fix, CrashId}, 120000).\\n\\nget_crashes() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, lists:sublist(lists:reverse(lists:keysort(3, All)), 10)\\n    end.\\n\\nclear_crashes() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, clear_crashes).\\n\\nreport_crash(Module, Reason, Stacktrace) ->\\n    CrashInfo = #{\\n        type => crash,\\n        module => Module,\\n        reason => Reason,\\n        stacktrace => Stacktrace,\\n        timestamp => erlang:system_time(millisecond)\\n    },\\n -> spawn_healer(CrashId)\\n    end,\\n    CrashId.\\n\\nstore_crash(Error, Stacktrace, Analysis) ->\\n    CrashId = generate_crash_id(),\\n    CrashData = maps:merge(#{\\n        id => CrashId,\\n        error => Error,\\n        stacktrace => Stacktrace,\\n        timestamp => erlang:system_time(millisecond)\\n    }, Analysis),\\n    ets:insert(?CRASH_TABLE, {CrashId, CrashData}),\\n end.\\n\\ncleanup_old_crashes() ->\\n    case ets:info(?CRASH_TABLE, size) of\\n        N when N > ?MAX_CRASHES ->\\n            All = ets:tab2list(?CRASH_TABLE),\\n            Sorted = lists:keysort(3, All),\\n            {ToKeep, _ToDelete} = lists:split(?MAX_CRASHES, lists:reverse(Sorted)),\\n            ets:delete_all_objects(?CRASH_TABLE),\\n            [ets:insert(?CRASH_TABLE, E) || E <- ToKeep];\\n        _ -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\ndo_analyze_crash(Error, Stacktrace) ->\\n    ErrorStr = format_error(Error),\\n    StacktraceStr = format_stacktrace(Stacktrace),\\n\\n    #{error_type => classify_error(Error),\\n      error_message => ErrorStr,\\n      stacktrace => StacktraceStr,\\n      affected_modules => extract_modules(Stacktrace),\\n      suggested_fix => [Error]).\\n\\nformat_stacktrace(Stacktrace) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [Stacktrace]).\\n\\nclassify_error({badarg, _}) -> badarg;\\nclassify_error({badmatch, _}) -> _}) -> process_not_found;\\nclassify_error({timeout, _}) -> timeout;\\nclassify_error({exit, _}) -> exit_signal;\\nclassify_error({error, Reason}) -> classify_error(Reason);\\nclassify_error(error) -> error;\\nclassify_error(Reason) when is_atom(Reason) -> Reason;\\nclassify_error(_) -> unknown.\\n\\nextract_modules([]) -> [];\\nextract_modules([{M, _, _, _} | Rest]) ->\\n    [M | ->\\n    Type = classify_error(Error),\\n    Modules = extract_modules(Stacktrace),\\n    \\n    % Check if we can rollback\\n    RollbackAvailable = can_rollback(Modules),\\n    \\n    case Type of\\n        badarg ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(check_arguments, Modules, \\n                \\\"Check function arguments - invalid type or value passed\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        badmatch ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(fix_pattern_match, Modules,\\n                \\\"Pattern match failed - verify expected values match actual\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        case_clause ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(add_case_clause, Modules,\\n                \\\"Missing case clause - add handling for unexpected value\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        function_clause ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(fix_function_arity, Modules,\\n                \\\"No matching function clause - check arity or add clause\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        undefined_function ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(export_or_define_function, Modules,\\n                \\\"Function not found - add -export or define function\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        process_not_found ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(check_process_start, Modules,\\n                \\\"Process not found - ensure dependent process is started\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n    exit_signal ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Process exited - check linked process or exit reason\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        error ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Error occurred - manual investigation required\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        _ ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Unknown error type - manual investigation required\\\", RollbackAvailable)\\n    end.\\n\\nsuggest_with_rollback(Action, Modules, Hint, true) ->\\n    #{action => Action, modules => Modules, hint => Hint, \\n      rollback_available => true, rollback_hint => \\\"Can auto-rollback to previous version\\\"};\\nsuggest_with_rollback(Action, Modules, Hint, false) ->\\n    #{action => Action, modules => Modules, hint => Hint,\\n      rollback_available => false, rollback_hint => \\\"No previous ]).\\n\\nformat_stacktrace_for_report(Stacktrace) when is_list(Stacktrace) ->\\n    format_stacktrace_list(Stacktrace);\\nformat_stacktrace_for_report(Stacktrace) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", Timestamp}]\\n-define(VERSIONS_DIR, \\\".tarha/versions\\\").\\n-define(CHECKPOINT_DIR, \\\".tarha/checkpoints\\\").\\n-define(MAX_VERSIONS, 5).  % Keep last 5 versions per module\\n-define(MODULES, [coding_agent_app, coding_agent_sup, coding_agent_ollama, coding_agent_tools, coding_agent, \\n                  coding_agent_session_sup, coding_agent_session, coding_agent_stream, coding_agent_lsp, \\n                  coding_agent_index, coding_agent_self, coding_agent_healer, coding_agent_process_monitor,\\n                  coding_agent_conv_memory, coding_agent_skills, coding_agent_http, coding_agent_repl]).\\n\\nstart_link() -> gen_server:start_link({local, ?MODULE}, ?MODULE, [], []).\\nreload_module(M) -> reload_module(M, #{rollback_on_crash => true}).\\nreload_module(M, Opts) -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, {reload_module, M, Opts}).\\nreload_all() -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, reload_all, 120000).\\nrollback(M) -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, {rollback, M}).\\nrollback_latest() -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, rollback_latest).\\nget_modules() -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, get_modules).\\nget_versions(M) -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, {get_versions, M}).\\nanalyze_self() -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, analyze_self, 60000).\\ncreate_checkpoint() -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, create_checkpoint).\\nrestore_checkpoint(Id) -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, {restore_checkpoint, Id}).\\nlist_checkpoints() -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, list_checkpoints).\\n\\ninit([]) ->\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(?VERSIONS_DIR ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(?CHECKPOINT_DIR ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    {ok, #state{}}.\\n\\nhandle_call({reload_module, M, Opts}, _From, State) -> \\n    {Reply, NewState} = do_reload_with_version(M, Opts, State),\\n    {reply, Reply, NewState};\\nhandle_call(reload_all, _From, State) -> \\n    {Results, NewState} = lists:mapfoldl(fun(M, S) -> \\n        {Reply, S2} = do_reload_with_version(M, #{}, S), \\n        {{M, Reply}, S2} \\n    end, State, ?MODULES),\\n    {reply, Results, NewState};\\nhandle_call({rollback, M}, _From, State) -> \\n    {Reply, NewState} = do_rollback(M, State),\\n    {reply, Reply, NewState};\\nhandle_call(rollback_latest, _From, State) ->\\n    {Reply, NewState} = do_rollback_latest(State),\\n    {reply, Reply, NewState};\\nhandle_call(get_modules, _From, S) -> {reply, [mod_info(M) || M <- ?MODULES], S};\\nhandle_call({get_versions, M}, _From, State) -> \\n    Versions = maps:get(M, State#state.versions, []),\\n    {reply, Versions, State};\\nhandle_call(analyze_self, _From, S) -> {reply, analyze(), S};\\nhandle_call(create_checkpoint, _From, S) -> {reply, checkpoint(), S};\\nhandle_call({restore_checkpoint, Id}, _From, S) -> {reply, restore(Id), S};\\nhandle_call(list_checkpoints, _From, S) -> {reply, checkpoints(), S};\\nhandle_call(_, _From, S) -> {reply, {error, unknown}, S}.\\n\\nhandle_cast(_, S) -> {noreply, S}.\\nhandle_info(_, S) -> {noreply, S}.\\nterminate(_, _) -> ok.\\ncode_change(_, S, _) -> {ok, S}.\\n\\n%% Versioned reload with automatic backup\\n\\ndo_reload_with_version(M, Opts, State) ->\\n    case code:which(M) of\\n        non_existing ->\\n            {{error, module_not_loaded}, State};\\n        CurrentBeam ->\\n            % Archive current version\\n            ArchiveResult = archive_version(M, CurrentBeam),\\n            case ArchiveResult of\\n                {ok, ArchivedPath} ->\\n                    % Load new version\\n                    case code:load_file(M) of\\n                        {module, M} ->\\n                            % Update version tracking\\n                            Timestamp = erlang:system_time(millisecond),\\n                            Versions = maps:get(M, State#state.versions, []),\\n                            NewVersions = [{ArchivedPath, Timestamp} | Versions],\\n                            TrimmedVersions = lists:sublist(NewVersions, ?MAX_VERSIONS),\\n                            NewState = State#state{versions = maps:put(M, TrimmedVersions, State#state.versions)},\\n                            \\n                            % Setup crash monitoring if requested\\n                            case maps:get(rollback_on_crash, Opts, true) of\\n                                true -> setup_rollback_monitor(M, ArchivedPath);\\n                                false -> ok\\n                            end,\\n                            \\n                            io:format(\\\"[self] Reloaded ~p (archived: ~s)~n\\\", [M, ArchivedPath]),\\n                            {#{success => true, module => M, archived => ArchivedPath}, NewState};\\n                        {error, Reason} ->\\n                            io:format(\\\"[self] Failed to reload ~p: ~p~n\\\", [M, Reason]),\\n                            {{error, Reason}, State}\\n                    end;\\n                {error, Reason} ->\\n                    io:format(\\\"[self] Failed to archive ~p: ~p~n\\\", [M, Reason]),\\n                    % Try to load anyway\\n                    case code:load_file(M) of\\n                        {module, M} -> {#{success => true, module => M, archived => false}, State};\\n                        {error, Reason} -> {{error, Reason}, State}\\n                    end\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\narchive_version(M, BeamPath) ->\\n    Timestamp = integer_to_binary(erlang:system_time(millisecond)),\\n    VersionDir = filename:join(?VERSIONS_DIR, atom_to_list(M)),\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(VersionDir ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    VersionPath = filename:join(VersionDir, binary_to_list(<<\\\"v\\\", Timestamp/binary, \\\".beam\\\">>)),\\n    case file:copy(BeamPath, VersionPath) of\\n        {ok, _} -> {ok, list_to_binary(VersionPath)};\\n        {error, Reason} -> {error, Reason}\\n    end.\\n\\nsetup_rollback_monitor(M, ArchivedPath) ->\\n    % Store archived path in process dictionary for crash recovery\\n    put({rollback_version, M}, ArchivedPath),\\n    ok.\\n\\n%% Rollback to previous version\\n\\ndo_rollback(M, State) ->\\n    Versions = maps:get(M, State#state.versions, []),\\n    case Versions of\\n        [] -> \\n            {{error, no_previous_version}, State};\\n        [{ArchivedPath, _Timestamp} | Rest] ->\\n            case restore_version(M, ArchivedPath) of\\n                ok ->\\n                    io:format(\\\"[self] Rolled back ~p to ~s~n\\\", [M, ArchivedPath]),\\n                    NewVersions = maps:put(M, Rest, State#state.versions),\\n                    {#{success => true, module => M, restored => ArchivedPath}, State#state{versions = NewVersions}};\\n                {error, Reason} ->\\n                    io:format(\\\"[self] Rollback failed for ~p: ~p~n\\\", [M, Reason]),\\n                    {{error, Reason}, State}\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\ndo_rollback_latest(State) ->\\n    % Find the module with the most recent crash\\n    AllVersions = lists:flatten([\\n        [{M, Path, Ts} || {Path, Ts} <- Versions]\\n        || {M, Versions} <- maps:to_list(State#state.versions)\\n    ]),\\n    case AllVersions of\\n        [] -> {{error, no_versions}, State};\\n        _ ->\\n            % Sort by timestamp (newest first)\\n            Sorted = lists:sort(fun({_, _, Ts1}, {_, _, Ts2}) -> Ts1 > Ts2 end, AllVersions),\\n            [{M, Path, _} | _] = Sorted,\\n            do_rollback(M, State)\\n    end.\\n\\nrestore_version(M, VersionPath) ->\\n    case filelib:is_file(VersionPath) of\\n        true ->\\n            % Purge current version\\n            code:soft_purge(M),\\n            % Load archived version\\n            case code:load_abs(filename:rootname(VersionPath)) of\\n                {module, M} -> ok;\\n                {error, Reason} -> {error, Reason}\\n            end;\\n        false ->\\n            {error, version_not_found}\\n    end.\\n\\n%% Module info\\n\\nmod_info(M) ->\\n    #{\\n        name => M, \\n        loaded => code:is_loaded(M) =/= false,\\n        path => case code:which(M) of \\n            non_existing -> undefined; \\n            P -> list_to_binary(P) \\n        end,\\n        current_version => get_current_version(M)\\n    }.\\n\\nget_current_version(M) ->\\n    Versions = case whereis(?MODULE) of\\n        undefined -> [];\\n        _ -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, {get_versions, M})\\n    end,\\n    case Versions of\\n        [{Path, _} | _] -> Path;\\n        _ -> <<>>\\n    end.\\n\\nanalyze() ->\\n    #{modules => [analyze_mod(M) || M <- ?MODULES], \\n      versions_dir => #{module => M, loaded => false}\\n    end.\\n\\n%% Checkpoint system (full snapshots)\\n\\ncheckpoint() ->\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(?CHECKPOINT_DIR ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    Id = integer_to_binary(erlang:system_time(millisecond)),\\n    Dir = filename:join(?CHECKPOINT_DIR, binary_to_list(Id)),\\n    file:make_dir(Dir),\\n    [backup_mod(M, Dir) || M <- ?MODULES],\\n    #{success => true, id => Id}.\\n\\nbackup_mod(M, Dir) ->\\n    case code:which(M) of\\n        Beam when is_list(Beam) -> file:copy(Beam, filename:join(Dir, filename:basename(Beam)));\\n        _ -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\nrestore(Id) ->\\n    Dir = filename:join(?CHECKPOINT_DIR, binary_to_list(Id)),\\n    case filelib:is_dir(Dir) of\\n        false -> #{success => false, error => <<\\\"Checkpoint not found\\\">>};\\n        true ->\\n            [restore_mod(M, Dir) || M <- ?MODULES],\\n            #{success => true}\\n    end.\\n\\nrestore_mod(M, Dir) ->\\n    Beam = filename:join(Dir, You CAN and SHOULD take multiple actions to complete tasks without asking for permission between steps.\\n\\n## Your Capabilities\\n\\nYou have access to tools for:\\n- Reading, writing, editing files\\n- Running bash commands and build tools\\n- Searching code with grep and file patterns\\n- Working with git (status, diff, commit, etc.)\\n\\n## How to Work\\n\\n1. **PLAN FIRST**: Before acting, briefly think through your approach\\n2. **EXECUTE AUTONOMOUSLY**: Take multiple actions in sequence without waiting for user confirmation\\n3. **VERIFY**: After changes, check that they work (run tests, build, lint)\\n4. **REPORT**: When done, summarize what you did\\n\\n## Multi-Step Workflows\\n\\nFor nontrivial tasks, you should:\\n- Read relevant files to understand context (use the Glob tool to find files)\\n- Make changes incrementally\\n- Test/verify after changes\\n- Report results\\n\\n## Tool Selection\\n\\n- Use `read_file` before `edit_file` (always read first)\\n- Use `edit_file` for targeted fixes, `write_file` for new files\\n- Use `bash` for running tests, builds, git commands\\n- Use `grep` to search for patterns\\n- Use `glob` to find files by pattern\\n\\n## Important Rules\\n\\n- ALWAYS use absolute paths when reading/writing files\\n- After editing files, suggest running relevant tests/linters\\n- For git commits, check status and diff first\\n- If a task requires multiple steps, do them all autonomously\\n- When genuinely stuck or need clarification, ask the user\\n\\n## Context\\n\\nWorking directory will be provided in the system context.\\nAlways use absolute paths when reading or writing files.\\\">>).\\n\\n-define(SKILL_PROMPT, <<\\\"# Skills\\n\\nYou have access to skills that provide specialized knowledge. }}.\\n\\nhandle_call({ask, Message, _Opts}, _From, State = #state{model = Model, messages = History, working_dir = WD, id = Id, open_files = OpenFiles}) ->\\n    MsgBin = iolist_to_binary(Message),\\n {error, Reason} ->\\n            {reply, {error, Reason}, State}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_call(history, _From, State = #state{messages = Messages}) ->\\n    {reply, {ok, Messages}, ok -> {reply, {ok, Id}, State};\\n        {error, Reason} -> {reply, {error, Reason}, State}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_call({restore_state, Data}, _From, _State) ->\\n    NewState = #state{\\n        id {noreply, State}.\\n\\nterminate(_Reason, #state{id = Id}) ->\\n    ets:delete(?SESSIONS_TABLE, Id),\\n    ok.\\n\\ncode_change(_OldVsn, State, _Extra) ->\\n    {ok, <<>>),\\n    AssistantMsg = #{\\n        <<\\\"role\\\">> => <<\\\"assistant\\\">>,\\n        <<\\\"content\\\">> => maps:get(<<\\\"content\\\">>, ResponseMsg, <<\\\"\\\">>),\\n        <<\\\"tool_calls\\\">> => ToolCalls\\n    },\\n    UpdatedMessages = Messages ++ [AssistantMsg],\\n    {ToolResults, NewOpenFiles} = execute_tool_calls(ToolCalls, OpenFiles),\\n    ToolMsg =   end;\\n\\nhandle_response(_Model, Messages, #{<<\\\"content\\\">> := Content} = ResponseMsg, _Iteration, OpenFiles) when Content =/= <<>>, Content =/= nil ->\\n    Thinking = E) || E <- ToKeep];\\n        _ -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\ndo_analyze_crash(Error, Stacktrace) ->\\n    ErrorStr = format_error(Error),\\n    StacktraceStr = format_stacktrace(Stacktrace),\\n\\n    #{error_type => classify_error(Error),\\n      error_message => ErrorStr,\\n      stacktrace => StacktraceStr,\\n      affected_modules => extract_modules(Stacktrace),\\n      suggested_fix => suggest_fix(Error, Stacktrace)}.\\n\\nformat_error({Reason, Stacktrace}) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p~n~p\\\", [Reason, Stacktrace]);\\nformat_error(Error) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [Error]).\\n\\nformat_stacktrace(Stacktrace) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [Stacktrace]).\\n\\nclassify_error({badarg, _}) -> badarg;\\nclassify_error({badmatch, _}) -> _}) -> process_not_found;\\nclassify_error({timeout, _}) -> timeout;\\nclassify_error({exit, _}) -> exit_signal;\\nclassify_error({error, Reason}) -> classify_error(Reason);\\nclassify_error(error) -> error;\\nclassify_error(Reason) when is_atom(Reason) -> Reason;\\nclassify_error(_) -> unknown.\\n\\nextract_modules([]) -> [];\\nextract_modules([{M, _, _, _} | Rest]) ->\\n    [M | extract_modules(Rest)];\\nextract_modules([{M, _, _} | Rest]) ->\\n    [M | extract_modules(Rest)];\\nextract_modules([_ | Rest]) ->\\n    extract_modules(Rest).\\n\\nsuggest_fix(Error, Stacktrace) of\\n        badarg ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(check_arguments, Modules, \\n                \\\"Check function arguments - invalid type or value passed\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        badmatch ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(fix_pattern_match, Modules,\\n                \\\"Pattern match failed - verify expected values match actual\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        case_clause ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(add_case_clause, Modules,\\n                \\\"Missing case clause - add handling for unexpected value\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        function_clause ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(fix_function_arity, Modules,\\n                \\\"No matching function clause - check arity or add clause\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        undefined_function ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(export_or_define_function, Modules,\\n                \\\"Function not found - add -export or define function\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        process_not_found ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(check_process_start, Modules,\\n                \\\"Process not found - ensure dependent process is started\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        timeout ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(increase_timeout_or_fix_hang, Modules,\\n                \\\"Operation timed out - increase timeout or fix blocking code\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        exit_signal ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Process exited - check linked process or exit reason\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        error ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Error occurred - manual investigation required\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        _ ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Unknown error type - manual investigation required\\\", RollbackAvailable)\\n    end.\\n\\nsuggest_with_rollback(Action, Modules, Hint, true) ->\\n    #{action => Action, modules => Modules, hint => Hint, \\n      rollback_available => true, rollback_hint => \\\"Can auto-rollback to previous     rollback_modules(Rest)\\n    end.\\n\\nfix_case_clause(CrashData) ->\\n    #{stacktrace := Stacktrace} = CrashData,\\n    case Stacktrace of\\n        [{M, F, A, _Loc} | _] ->\\n <<\"-module(coding_agent_process_monitor).\\n-behaviour(gen_server).\\n-export([start_link/0, status/0, trim/0, trim/1, gc/0, gc/1, set_limit/1, get_limit/0]).\\n-export([monitor_process/1, {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info({large_heap, Pid, Size}, State) ->\\n    io:format(\\\"[memory] Large heap detected: ~p using ~p bytes~n\\\", [Pid, Size]),\\n    auto_cleanup(Pid, Size, State),\\n    {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info(gc_check, State) ->\\n    CurrentMemory = erlang:memory(total),\\n    case CurrentMemory > State#state.memory_limit of\\n        true ->\\n            io:format(\\\"[memory] Memory limit exceeded: ~p > ~p, trimming~n\\\", [CurrentMemory, State#state.memory_limit]),\\n            do_memory_trim(all);\\n        false ->\\n            ok\\n    end,\\n {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info({large_heap, Pid, Size}, State) ->\\n    io:format(\\\"[memory] Large heap detected: ~p using ~p bytes~n\\\", [Pid, Size]),\\n    auto_cleanup(Pid, Size, State),\\n    {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info(gc_check, State) ->\\n    CurrentMemory = erlang:memory(total),\\n    case CurrentMemory > State#state.memory_limit of\\n        true ->\\n State#state{monitored_pids = NewMonitored}};\\n        error ->\\n            {noreply, State}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_info(_Info, State) ->\\n    {noreply, State}.\\n\\nterminate(_Reason, _State) ->\\n    ok.\\n\\ncode_change(_OldVsn, State, _Extra) ->\\n    {ok, State}.\\n\\nstatus() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, status).\\n\\ntrim() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, trim).\\n\\ntrim(What) ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, {trim, What}).\\n\\ngc() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, gc).\\n\\ngc(What) ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, {gc, gen_server:call(?MODULE, {monitor_process, Pid}).\\n\\nunmonitor_process(Pid) ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, {unmonitor_process, Pid}).\\n\\nget_monitored() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, get_monitored).\\n\\nschedule_gc_check() ->\\n    erlang:send_after(60000, self(), gc_check).\\n\\ngather_memory_status() ->\\n    Processes = erlang:processes(),\\n    ProcInfo =        {true, #{\\n                    pid => Pid,\\n                    memory => Mem,\\n                    queue_len => QLen,\\n                    heap_size => Heap,\\n                    name =>      {registered_name, Name} when is_atom(Name) -> Name;\\n        _ -> Pid\\n    end.\\n\\ndo_memory_trim(all) ->\\n    try\\n        trim_sessions(),\\n        trim_ets_tables(),\\n ->\\n            case maps:get(Pid, Monitored, undefined) of\\n                undefined ->\\n                    Ref = monitor(process, Pid),\\n                    NewMonitored = Monitored#{Pid => CrashInfo = #{\\n        type => exit,\\n        pid => Pid,\\n        reason => Reason,\\n        stacktrace => Stacktrace,\\n        timestamp => erlang:system_time(millisecond)\\n    },\\n    CrashId = store_crash(exit, Reason, CrashInfo),\\n    case State#state.auto_heal of\\n        true -> spawn_healer(CrashId);\\n        false -> ok\\n    end,\\n    {noreply, gen_server:call(?MODULE, get_crashes).\\n\\nget_recent_crashes() ->\\n    case ets:whereis(?CRASH_TABLE) of\\n        undefined -> [];\\n        Table ->\\n            All = ets:tab2list(Table),\\n            lists:sublist(lists:reverse(lists:keysort(3, All)), 10)\\n    end.\\n\\nclear_crashes() ->\\n    gen_server:call(?MODULE, clear_crashes).\\n\\nreport_crash(Module, Reason, Stacktrace) ->\\n    CrashInfo = #{\\n        type => crash,\\n        module => Module,\\n        reason => Reason,\\n        stacktrace => Stacktrace,\\n        timestamp => erlang:system_time(millisecond)\\n    },\\n #{error_type => classify_error(Error),\\n      error_message => ErrorStr,\\n      stacktrace => StacktraceStr,\\n      affected_modules => extract_modules(Stacktrace),\\n      suggested_fix => suggest_fix(Error, Stacktrace)}.\\n\\nformat_error({Reason, Stacktrace}) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p~n~p\\\", [Reason, Stacktrace]);\\nformat_error(Error) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [Error]).\\n\\nformat_stacktrace(Stacktrace) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [Stacktrace]).\\n\\nclassify_error({badarg, _}) -> badarg;\\nclassify_error({badmatch, _}) -> _}) -> process_not_found;\\nclassify_error({timeout, _}) -> timeout;\\nclassify_error({exit, _}) -> exit_signal;\\nclassify_error({error, Reason}) -> classify_error(Reason);\\nclassify_error(error) -> error;\\nclassify_error(Reason) when is_atom(Reason) -> Reason;\\nclassify_error(_) -> unknown.\\n\\nextract_modules([]) -> [];\\nextract_modules([{M, _, _, _} | Rest]) ->\\n    [M | extract_modules(Rest)];\\nextract_modules([{M, _, _} | Rest]) ->\\n    [M | extract_modules(Rest)];\\nextract_modules([_ | Rest]) ->\\n    extract_modules(Rest).\\n\\nsuggest_fix(Error, Stacktrace) ->\\n    Type = classify_error(Error),\\n    Modules = extract_modules(Stacktrace),\\n    \\n    % Check if we can rollback\\n    RollbackAvailable = can_rollback(Modules),\\n    \\n    case Type of\\n        badarg ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(check_arguments, Modules, \\n                \\\"Check function arguments - invalid type or value passed\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        badmatch ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(fix_pattern_match, Modules,\\n                \\\"Pattern match failed - verify expected values match actual\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        case_clause ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(add_case_clause, Modules,\\n                \\\"Missing case clause - add handling for unexpected value\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        function_clause ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(fix_function_arity, Modules,\\n                \\\"No matching function clause - check arity or add clause\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        undefined_function ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(export_or_define_function, Modules,\\n                \\\"Function not found - add -export or define function\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        process_not_found ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(check_process_start, Modules,\\n                \\\"Process not found - ensure dependent process is started\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n    exit_signal ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Process exited - check linked process or exit reason\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        error ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Error occurred - manual investigation required\\\", RollbackAvailable);\\n        _ ->\\n            suggest_with_rollback(investigate, Modules,\\n                \\\"Unknown error type - manual investigation required\\\", RollbackAvailable)\\n    end.\\n\\nsuggest_with_rollback(Action, Modules, version\\\"};\\nsuggest_with_rollback(Action, Modules, Hint, false) ->\\n    #{action => Action, modules => Modules, hint => Hint,\\n      rollback_available => false, rollback_hint => \\\"No previous version available\\\"}.\\n\\ncan_rollback([]) -> false;\\ncan_rollback([M | _]) ->\\n    case whereis(coding_agent_self) of\\n        undefined -> false;\\n        _ ->\\n            case coding_agent_self:get_versions(M) of\\n                [_ | _] -> true;\\n                _ -> false\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\nattempt_auto_fix(CrashData) ->\\n    #{analysis := Analysis} = CrashData,\\n    #{suggested_fix := Suggestion} = Analysis,\\n\\n    case maps:get(action, Suggestion, none) of\\n        none ->\\n            {error, no_auto_fix_available};\\n        Action ->\\n            case try_apply_fix(Action, CrashData) of\\n                {ok, Result} ->\\n                    % Write fix report\\n                    write_fix_report(CrashData, Action, Result),\\n                    {ok, #{fix_applied => Action, result => Result}};\\n                {error, Reason} ->\\n                    {error, Reason}\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\nwrite_crash_report(CrashId) Filename};\\n                {error, Reason} ->\\n                    {error, Reason}\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\ngenerate_crash_report_content(CrashId, CrashData) ->\\n    Timestamp = Stacktrace = maps:get(stacktrace, CrashData, []),\\n    Analysis = maps:get(analysis, CrashData, #{}),\\n    \\n    SuggestedFix = maps:get(suggested_fix, Analysis, #{}),\\n    AffectedModules = maps:get(affected_modules, Analysis, []),\\n    \\n    iolist_to_binary([\\n        <<\\\"# Crash Report\\\\n\\\\n\\\">>,\\n        io_lib:format(\\\"**Crash ID:** ~s\\\\n\\\\n\\\", [CrashId]),\\n ]).\\n\\nformat_stacktrace_for_report(Stacktrace) when is_list(Stacktrace) ->\\n    format_stacktrace_list(Stacktrace);\\nformat_stacktrace_for_report(Stacktrace) ->\\n    io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [Stacktrace]).\\n\\nformat_stacktrace_list([]) -> <<\\\"\\\">>;\\nformat_stacktrace_list([{M, F, A, Info} | Rest]) when is_list(A) ->\\n    Line = io_lib:format(\\\"  ~p:~p/~b at ~s:~p~n\\\", [\\n format_stacktrace_list(Rest).\\n\\nwrite_fix_report(CrashData, Action, Result) ->\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(?CRASH_REPORT_DIR ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    CrashId = maps:get(id, CrashData,     io_lib:format(\\\"**Crash ID:** ~s\\\\n\\\\n\\\", [CrashId]),\\n        io_lib:format(\\\"**Fix Applied:** ~p\\\\n\\\\n\\\", [Action]),\\n        io_lib:format(\\\"**Timestamp:** ~p\\\\n\\\\n\\\", If crash persists, run /fix again or investigate manually\\\\n\\\">>\\n    ]).\\n\\ntry_apply_fix(check_arguments, _CrashData) ->\\n    {error, manual_fix_required};\\ntry_apply_fix(fix_pattern_match, _CrashData) ->\\n    {error, manual_fix_required};\\ntry_apply_fix(add_case_clause, CrashData) ->\\n    fix_case_clause(CrashData);\\ntry_apply_fix(fix_function_arity, _CrashData) ->\\n    {error, #{affected_modules => []}),\\n    rollback_modules(Modules);\\ntry_apply_fix(_, _CrashData) ->\\n    {error, manual_fix_required}.\\n\\nrollback_modules([]) ->\\n    {error,     rollback_modules(Rest)\\n    end.\\n\\nfix_case_clause(CrashData) ->\\n    #{stacktrace := Stacktrace} = CrashData,\\n    case Stacktrace of\\n        [{M, F, A, _Loc} | _] ->\\n            SourceFile = find_source_file(M),\\n            case file:read_file(SourceFile) of\\n                {ok, Content} ->\\n                    case find_case_clause_location(Content, F, A) of\\n                        {ok, CaseStart, CaseEnd} ->\\n                            NewContent = add_catch_all_case(Content, CaseStart, CaseEnd),\\n                            file:write_file(SourceFile, NewContent),\\n                            coding_agent_self:reload_module(M),\\n                            {ok, #{file => SourceFile, action => added_catch_all}};\\n                        {error, not_found} ->\\n                            {error, could_not_locate_case}\\n                    end;\\n                {error, _} ->\\n                    {error, cannot_read_source}\\n            end;\\n        _ ->\\n            {error, invalid_stacktrace}\\n    end.\\n\\nfix_missing_function(CrashData) ->\\n    #{analysis := Analysis} = CrashData,\\n    #{affected_modules := Modules} = Analysis,\\n\\n    case Modules of\\n        [M | _] ->\\n            SourceFile = find_source_file(M),\\n            case file:read_file(SourceFile) of\\n                {ok, Content} ->\\n                    ExportSection = extract_exports(Content),\\n                    MissingFuncs = find_missing_exports(Content, ExportSection),\\n                    case MissingFuncs of\\n                        [] ->\\n                            {error, no_missing_exports_found};\\n                        _ ->\\n                            NewContent = add_to_exports(Content, MissingFuncs),\\n                            file:write_file(SourceFile, NewContent),\\n                            coding_agent_self:reload_module(M),\\n                            {ok, #{added_exports => MissingFuncs}}\\n                    end;\\n                {error, _} ->\\n                    {error, cannot_read_source}\\n            end;\\n        [] ->\\n            {error, no_affected_modules}\\n    end.\\n\\nfind_source_file(Module) ->\\n    case code:which(Module) of\\n        Beam when is_list(Beam) ->\\n            SrcFile = Beam ++ \\\".erl\\\",\\n            case filelib:is_file(SrcFile) of\\n                true -> SrcFile;\\n                false ->\\n                    SrcDir = filename:dirname(Beam),\\n                    SrcFile2 = filename:join([SrcDir, \\\"..\\\", \\\"src\\\", \\\".erl\\\")\\n    end.\\n\\nfind_case_clause_location(Content, _F, _A) ->\\n    Lines = binary:split(Content, <<\\\"\\\\n\\\">>, [global]),\\n    find_case_start(Lines, 1, none).\\n\\nfind_case_start([], _, none) -> {error, not_found};\\nfind_case_start([Line | Rest], LineNum, none) ->\\n    case binary:match(Line, <<\\\"case \\\">>) of\\n        {_, _} ->\\n            case find_case_end(Rest, LineNum + 1, 1) of\\n                {ok, EndLine} -> {ok, LineNum, EndLine};\\n                error -> find_case_start(Rest, LineNum + 1, none)\\n            end;\\n filename:join(?VERSIONS_DIR, atom_to_list(M)),\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(VersionDir ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    VersionPath = filename:join(VersionDir, binary_to_list(<<\\\"v\\\", Timestamp/binary, \\\".beam\\\">>)),\\n    case file:copy(BeamPath, VersionPath) of\\n        {ok, _} -> {ok, list_to_binary(VersionPath)};\\n        {error, Reason} -> {error, Reason}\\n    end.\\n\\nsetup_rollback_monitor(M, ArchivedPath) ->\\n    % Store archived path in process dictionary for crash recovery\\n    put({rollback_version, M}, ArchivedPath),\\n    ok.\\n\\n%% Rollback to previous version\\n\\ndo_rollback(M, State) ->\\n    Versions = maps:get(M, State#state.versions, []),\\n    case Versions of\\n        [] -> \\n            {{error, no_previous_version}, State};\\n        [{ArchivedPath, _Timestamp} | Rest] ->\\n            case restore_version(M, ArchivedPath) of\\n                ok ->\\n                    io:format(\\\"[self] Rolled back ~p to ~s~n\\\", [M, ArchivedPath]),\\n                    NewVersions = maps:put(M, Rest, State#state.versions),\\n                    {#{success => true, module => M, restored => ArchivedPath}, State#state{versions = NewVersions}};\\n                {error, Reason} ->\\n                    io:format(\\\"[self] Rollback failed for ~p: ~p~n\\\", [M, Reason]),\\n                    {{error, Reason}, State}\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\ndo_rollback_latest(State) ->\\n    % Find the module with the most recent crash\\n    AllVersions = lists:flatten([\\n        [{M, Path, Ts} || {Path, Ts} <- Versions]\\n        || {M, Versions} <- maps:to_list(State#state.versions)\\n    ]),\\n    case AllVersions of\\n        [] -> {{error, no_versions}, State};\\n        _ ->\\n            % Sort by timestamp (newest first)\\n            Sorted = lists:sort(fun({_, _, Ts1}, {_, _, Ts2}) -> Ts1 > Ts2 end, AllVersions),\\n            [{M, Path, _} | _] = Sorted,\\n            do_rollback(M, State)\\n    end.\\n\\nrestore_version(M, VersionPath) ->\\n    case filelib:is_file(VersionPath) of\\n        true ->\\n            % Purge current version\\n            code:soft_purge(M),\\n            % Load archived version\\n            case code:load_abs(filename:rootname(VersionPath)) of\\n                {module, M} -> ok;\\n                {error, Reason} -> {error, Reason}\\n            end;\\n        false ->\\n            {error, version_not_found}\\n    end.\\n\\n%% Module info\\n\\nmod_info(M) ->\\n    #{\\n        name => M, \\n        loaded => code:is_loaded(M) =/= false,\\n        path => case code:which(M) of \\n            non_existing -> undefined; \\n            P -> list_to_binary(P) \\n        end,\\n        current_version => get_current_version(M)\\n    }.\\n\\nget_current_version(M) ->\\n    Versions = case whereis(?MODULE) of\\n        undefined -> [];\\n        _ -> gen_server:call(?MODULE, {get_versions, M})\\n    end,\\n    case Versions of\\n        [{Path, _} | _] -> Path;\\n        _ -> <<>>\\n    end.\\n\\nanalyze() ->\\n    #{modules => [analyze_mod(M) || M <- ?MODULES], \\n      versions_dir => list_to_binary(?VERSIONS_DIR)}.\\n\\nanalyze_mod(M) ->\\n    case code:which(M) of\\n        Beam when is_list(Beam) -> #{module => M, loaded => true, path => list_to_binary(Beam)};\\n        _ -> #{module => M, loaded => false}\\n    end.\\n\\n%% Checkpoint system (full snapshots)\\n\\ncheckpoint() ->\\n    filelib:ensure_dir(?CHECKPOINT_DIR ++ \\\"/\\\"),\\n    Id = integer_to_binary(erlang:system_time(millisecond)),\\n    Dir = filename:join(?CHECKPOINT_DIR, binary_to_list(Id)),\\n    file:make_dir(Dir),\\n    [backup_mod(M, Dir) || M <- ?MODULES],\\n    #{success => true, id => Id}.\\n\\nbackup_mod(M, Dir) ->\\n    case code:which(M) of\\n        Beam when is_list(Beam) -> file:copy(Beam, filename:join(Dir, filename:basename(Beam)));\\n        _ -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\nrestore(Id) ->\\n    Dir = filename:join(?CHECKPOINT_DIR, binary_to_list(Id)),\\n    case filelib:is_dir(Dir) of\\n        false -> #{success => false, error => <<\\\"Checkpoint not found\\\">>};\\n        true ->\\n            [restore_mod(M, Dir) || M <- ?MODULES],\\n            #{success => true}\\n    end.\\n\\nrestore_mod(M, Dir) ->\\n    Beam = filename:join(Dir, atom_to_list(M) ++ \\\".beam\\\"),\\n    case filelib:is_file(Beam) of\\n        true -> code:soft_purge(M), code:load_abs(filename:rootname(Beam));\\n        false -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\ncheckpoints() You CAN and SHOULD take multiple actions to complete tasks without asking for permission between steps.\\n\\n## Your Capabilities\\n\\nYou have access to tools for:\\n- Reading, writing, editing files\\n- Running bash commands and build tools\\n- Searching code with grep and file patterns\\n- Working with git (status, diff, commit, etc.)\\n\\n## How to Work\\n\\n1. **PLAN FIRST**: Before acting, briefly think through your approach\\n2. **EXECUTE AUTONOMOUSLY**: Take multiple actions in sequence without waiting for user confirmation\\n3. **VERIFY**: After changes, check that they work (run tests, build, lint)\\n4. **REPORT**: When done, summarize what you did\\n\\n## Multi-Step Workflows\\n\\nFor nontrivial tasks, you should:\\n- Read relevant files to understand context (use the Glob tool to find files)\\n- Make changes incrementally\\n- Test/verify after changes\\n- Report results\\n\\n## Tool Selection\\n\\n- Use `read_file` before `edit_file` (always read first)\\n- Use `edit_file` for targeted fixes, `write_file` for new files\\n- Use `bash` for running tests, builds, git commands\\n- Use `grep` to search for patterns\\n- Use `glob` to find files by pattern\\n\\n## Important Rules\\n\\n- ALWAYS use absolute paths when reading/writing files\\n- After editing files, suggest running relevant tests/linters\\n- For git commits, check status and diff first\\n- If a task requires multiple steps, do them all autonomously\\n- When genuinely stuck or need clarification, ask the user\\n\\n## Context\\n\\nWorking directory will be provided in the system context.\\nAlways use absolute paths when reading or writing files.\\\">>).\\n\\n-define(SKILL_PROMPT, <<\\\"# Skills\\n\\nYou have access to skills that provide specialized knowledge. }}.\\n\\nhandle_call({ask, Message, _Opts}, _From, State = #state{model = Model, messages = History, working_dir = WD, id = Id, open_files = OpenFiles}) ->\\n    MsgBin = iolist_to_binary(Message),\\n    WDBin = list_to_binary(WD),\\n    \\n    % Build file context from open files\\n    FileContext = build_file_context(OpenFiles),\\n    \\n    % Get memory context\\n    MemoryContext = => <<\\\"system\\\">>, <<\\\"content\\\">> => SystemContent},\\n    UserMsg = #{<<\\\"role\\\">> => <<\\\"user\\\">>, <<\\\"content\\\">> => MsgBin},\\n    ExistingHistory = trim_history(History),\\n    Messages = [SystemMsg | ExistingHistory] ++ [UserMsg],\\n    \\n    case run_agent_loop(Model, Messages, 0, OpenFiles) of\\n        {ok, Response, Thinking, NewHistory, FinalOpenFiles, TokensUsed} ->\\n            FinalHistory = trim_history(NewHistory, ?MAX_HISTORY),\\n            ReplyHistory = [{maps:get(<<\\\"role\\\">>, M), maps:get(<<\\\"content\\\">>, M, <<\\\"\\\">>)} || M <- lists:sublist(FinalHistory, 2, length(FinalHistory))],\\n            NewState = State#state{\\n                messages = FinalHistory,\\n                open_files = FinalOpenFiles,\\n                total_tokens = State#state.total_tokens + TokensUsed,\\n                tool_calls = State#state.tool_calls + 1\\n            },\\n            % Check if consolidation needed (async)\\n            maybe_trigger_consolidation(),\\n            % Auto-save session (async)\\n            maybe_save_session(NewState),\\n            {reply, {ok, Response, Thinking, ReplyHistory}, NewState};\\n        {error, Reason} ->\\n            {reply, {error, Reason}, State}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_call(history, _From, State = #state{messages = Messages}) ->\\n    {reply, {ok, Messages}, <<\\\"total_tokens_estimate\\\">> => Tokens,\\n        <<\\\"tool_calls\\\">> => Calls,\\n        <<\\\"message_count\\\">> => length(State#state.messages)\\n    }}, State};\\n\\nhandle_call(clear, _From, State) ->\\n    {reply, ok, State#state{messages = [], open_files = #{}}};\\n\\nhandle_call(save_session, _From, State = #state{id = Id, model = Model, working_dir = WD, open_files = ok -> {reply, {ok, Id}, State};\\n        {error, Reason} -> {reply, {error, Reason}, State}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_call({restore_state, Data}, _From, _State) ->\\n    NewState = #state{\\n        id = maps:get(id, Data, <<>>),\\n        model = maps:get(model, Data, <<\\\"glm-5:cloud\\\">>),\\n        messages = maps:get(messages, Data, []),\\n        working_dir = case maps:get(working_dir, maps:get(open_files, Data, #{}),\\n        total_tokens = maps:get(total_tokens, Data, 0),\\n        tool_calls = maps:get(tool_calls, Data, 0)\\n    },\\n    {reply, ok, NewState};\\n\\nhandle_call(_Request, _From, State) ->\\n    {reply, {error, unknown_request}, State}.\\n\\nhandle_cast(_Msg, State) ->\\n    {noreply, State}.\\n\\nhandle_info(_Info, State) ->\\n    {noreply, State}.\\n\\nterminate(_Reason, #state{id = Id}) ->\\n    ets:delete(?SESSIONS_TABLE, Id),\\n    ok.\\n\\ncode_change(_OldVsn, State, _Extra) ->\\n    {ok, State}.\\n\\nbuild_file_context(OpenFiles) when map_size(OpenFiles) == 0 ->\\n    <<>>;\\nbuild_file_context(OpenFiles) ->\\n    maps:fold(fun(Path, Content, Acc) ->\\n        PathBin = iolist_to_binary(Path),\\n        case byte_size(Acc) + byte_size(Content) > 50000 of\\n            true -> Acc;\\n            false -> <<Acc/binary, \\\"\\\\n--- \\\", PathBin/binary, \\\" ---\\\\n\\\", Content/binary>>\\n        end\\n    end, <<>>, OpenFiles).\\n\\nrun_agent_loop(Model, Messages, Iteration, OpenFiles) when Iteration >= ?MAX_ITERATIONS ->\\n    {error, max_iterations_reached, Messages};\\nrun_agent_loop(Model, Messages, Iteration, OpenFiles) ->\\n    Tools = coding_agent_tools:tools(),\\n    case coding_agent_ollama:chat_with_tools(Model, Messages, Tools) of\\n        {ok, #{<<\\\"message\\\">> := ResponseMsg}} ->\\n            handle_response(Model, Messages, ResponseMsg, Iteration, OpenFiles);\\n        {error, Reason} ->\\n            {error, Reason}\\n    end.\\n\\nhandle_response(Model, Messages, #{<<\\\"tool_calls\\\">> := ToolCalls} = ResponseMsg, Iteration, OpenFiles) ->\\n    Thinking = maps:get(<<\\\"thinking\\\">>, ResponseMsg, <<>>),\\n    AssistantMsg = #{\\n        <<\\\"role\\\">> => <<\\\"assistant\\\">>,\\n        <<\\\"content\\\">> => maps:get(<<\\\"content\\\">>, ResponseMsg, <<\\\"\\\">>),\\n        <<\\\"tool_calls\\\">> => ToolCalls\\n    },\\n    UpdatedMessages = Messages ++ [AssistantMsg],\\n    {ToolResults, NewOpenFiles} = execute_tool_calls(ToolCalls, OpenFiles),\\n    ToolMsg = #{<<\\\"role\\\">> => <<\\\"tool\\\">>, <<\\\"content\\\">> => ToolResults},\\n    MessagesWithResults = UpdatedMessages ++ [ToolMsg],\\n    \\n    % Estimate tokens\\n    MsgSize = estimate_message_size(MessagesWithResults),\\n    \\n    case run_agent_loop(Model, MessagesWithResults, Iteration + 1, NewOpenFiles) of\\n        {ok, Response, NewThinking, NewHistory, FinalOpenFiles, TokensUsed} ->\\n            CombinedThinking = case Thinking of\\n                <<>> -> NewThinking;\\n                _ -> <<Thinking/binary, \\\"\\\\n\\\\n\\\", NewThinking/binary>>\\n            end,\\n            {ok, Response, CombinedThinking, NewHistory, FinalOpenFiles, TokensUsed + MsgSize};\\n        {error, Reason} ->\\n            {error, Reason}\\n    end;\\n\\nhandle_response(_Model, Messages, #{<<\\\"content\\\">> := Content} = ResponseMsg, _Iteration, OpenFiles) when Content =/= <<>>, Content =/= nil ->\\n    Thinking = maps:get(<<\\\"thinking\\\">>, ResponseMsg, <<>>),\\n    AssistantMsg = #{<<\\\"role\\\">> => <<\\\"assistant\\\">>, <<\\\"content\\\">> => Content},\\n    NewHistory = Messages ++ [AssistantMsg],\\n    MsgSize = estimate_message_size(NewHistory),\\n    {ok, Content, Thinking, NewHistory, OpenFiles, MsgSize};\\n\\nhandle_response(_Model, _Messages, _ResponseMsg, _Iteration, _OpenFiles) ->\\n    {error, unexpected_response}.\\n\\nestimate_message_size(Messages) ->\\n    lists:foldl(fun(Msg, Acc) ->\\n        Content = maps:get(<<\\\"content\\\">>, Msg, <<\\\"\\\">>),\\n        Acc + byte_size(Content)\\n    end, 0, Messages).\\n\\nexecute_tool_calls(ToolCalls, OpenFiles) when is_list(ToolCalls) ->\\n    Results = [execute_single_tool_with_retry(TC, OpenFiles) || TC <- ToolCalls],\\n    NewOpenFiles = lists:foldl(fun\\n        ({{#{<<\\\"success\\\">> := true, <<\\\"file_cached\\\">> := Path, <<\\\"content\\\">> := Content}}, _}, Acc) ->\\n            maps:put(Path, Content, Acc);\\n        ({#{<<\\\"success\\\">> := true, <<\\\"file_opened\\\">> := Path}, _}, Acc) ->\\n            % Remove from cache since content changed\\n            maps:remove(Path, Acc);\\n        (_, Acc) -> Acc\\n    end, OpenFiles, Results),\\n    ResultList = [R || {R, _} <- Results],\\n    {list_to_binary(io_lib:format(\\\"~p\\\", [ResultList])), RetryCount >= ?MAX_TOOL_RETRIES ->\\n    % Max retries reached, return failure\\n    {#{<<\\\"success\\\">> => false, <<\\\"error\\\">> => <<\\\"Max retries exceeded\\\">>}, OpenFiles};\\nexecute_single_tool_with_retry(TC, OpenFiles, RetryCount) ->\\n    case execute_single_tool(TC, OpenFiles) of\\n        {#{<<\\\"success\\\">> := false, <<\\\"error\\\">> := Error} = Result, NewOpenFiles} ->\\n            % Retry on failure\\n            case should_retry(Error) of\\n                true ->\\n                    timer:sleep(100 * (RetryCount + 1)),  % Exponential backoff\\n                    execute_single_tool_with_retry(TC, NewOpenFiles, RetryCount + 1);\\n                false ->\\n                    {Result, NewOpenFiles}\\n            end;\\n        Success ->\\n            Success\\n    end.\\n\\nshould_retry(<<\\\"file not found\\\">>) -> false;\\nshould_retry(<<\\\"permission denied\\\">>) -> false;\\nshould_retry(<<\\\"syntax error\\\">>) -> false;\\nshould_retry(_) -> true.  % Retry on transient errors\\n\\nexecute_single_tool(#{<<\\\"function\\\">> := #{<<\\\"name\\\">> := Name, <<\\\"arguments\\\">> := Args}}, OpenFiles) ->\\n    Result = coding_agent_tools:execute(Name, Args),\\n    \\n    % Cache file content if it was read successfully\\n    CachedResult = case Name of\\n        <<\\\"read_file\\\">> ->\\n            case Result of\\n                #{<<\\\"success\\\">> := true, <<\\\"content\\\">> := Content} ->\\n                    Path = maps:get(<<\\\"path\\\">>, Args),\\n                    Result#{<<\\\"file_cached\\\">> => Path};\\n                _ -> Result\\n            end;\\n        <<\\\"write_file\\\">> ->\\n            case Result of\\n                #{<<\\\"success\\\">> := true} ->\\n                    Path = maps:get(<<\\\"path\\\">>, Args),\\n                    % Remove from cache since content changed\\n                    Result#{<<\\\"file_opened\\\">> => Path};\\n                _ -> Result\\n            end;\\n        <<\\\"edit_file\\\">> ->\\n            case Result of\\n                #{<<\\\"success\\\">> := true} ->\\n                    Path = maps:get(<<\\\"path\\\">>, Args),\\n                    % Remove from cache since content changed\\n                    Result#{<<\\\"file_opened\\\">> => Path};\\n                _ -> Result\\n            end;\\n        _ -> Result\\n    end,\\n    {CachedResult, OpenFiles}.\\n\\ngenerate_id() ->\\n    <<A:32, B:32, C:32>> = crypto:strong_rand_bytes(12),\\n    iolist_to_binary(io_lib:format(\\\"~8.16.0b-~8.16.0b-~8.16.0b\\\", [A, B, C])).\\n\\ntrim_history(History) ->\\n    trim_history(History, ?MAX_TOKENS).\\n\\ntrim_history(History, MaxTokens) ->\\n    HistorySize = coding_agent_ollama:count_tokens(History),\\n    case HistorySize > MaxTokens of\\n        false -> History;\\n        true ->\\n            % Remove oldest messages until we're under limit\\n            % Keep system message (first) and last message\\n            case length(History) of\\n                N when N =< 2 -> History;\\n                _ ->\\n                    % Remove the oldest non-system message\\n                    [SysMsg | Rest] = History,\\n                    case Rest of\\n                        [] -> [SysMsg];\\n                        [Last] -> <<\"-module(coding_agent_process_monitor).\\n-behaviour(gen_server).\\n-export([start_link/0, status/0, trim/0, trim/1, gc/0, gc/1, set_limit/1, get_limit/0]).\\n-export([monitor_process/1,   {reply, {ok, Ref}, State#state{monitored_pids = NewMonitored}};\\n\\nhandle_call({unmonitor_process, Pid}, _From, State = #state{monitored_pids = Monitored}) ->\\n    case maps:find(Pid, Monitored) {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info({large_heap, Pid, Size}, State) ->\\n    io:format(\\\"[memory] Large heap detected: ~p using ~p bytes~n\\\", [Pid, Size]),\\n    auto_cleanup(Pid, Size, State),\\n    {noreply, State};\\n\\nhandle_info(gc_check, State) ->\\n    CurrentMemory = erlang:memory(total),\\n    case CurrentMemory > State#state.memory_limit of\\n        true ->\\n            io:format(\\\"[memory] Memory limit exceeded: ~p > ~p, trimming~n\\\", [CurrentMemory, State#state.memory_limit]),\\n            do_memory_trim(all);\\n        false ->\\n            ok\\n    end,\\n      {registered_name, Name} when is_atom(Name) -> Name;\\n        _ -> Pid\\n    end.\\n\\ndo_memory_trim(all) ->\\n    try\\n        trim_sessions(),\\n        trim_ets_tables(),\\n {Type, Error}, \\n                        Stacktrace\\n                    )\\n            end,\\n            {error, {Type, Error}}\\n    end;\\ndo_memory_trim(sessions) ->\\n    trim_sessions(),\\n       undefined -> ok;\\n        Table ->\\n            try\\n                AllSessions = ets:tab2list(Table),\\n                Now = erlang:system_time(millisecond),\\n                OldThreshold                                  undefined -> ok;\\n                                        Pid when is_pid(Pid) -> catch gen_server:stop(Pid)\\n                                    end;\\n                                _ -> ok\\n                            end;\\n                        _ -> ok\\n                    end\\n                end, AllSessions)\\n            catch\\n                _:_ -> ok\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\nclear_session_caches() ->\\n    Sessions = get_all_session_pids(),\\n    [catch gen_server:call(Pid, clear, 5000) || Pid <- ~p has ~p queued messages, killing~n\\\", [Pid, N]),\\n            exit(Pid, kill);\\n        _ ->\\n            ok\\n    end.\\n\\nget_all_session_pids() ->\\n    case   catch\\n                _:_ -> []\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\ntrim_ets_tables() ->\\n    AllTables = ets:all(),\\n    [try trim_one_ets_table(T) catch _:_ -> ok end || T <-           % Keep most recent entries if possible\\n            case ets:info(Table, type) of\\n                ordered_set ->\\n                    % Ordered set - delete oldest\\n                    Sorted = ets:tab2list(Table),\\n                    case length(Sorted) > 1000 of\\n                        true ->\\n                            {ToKeep, _} = lists:split(1000, lists:reverse(Sorted)),\\n                            ets:delete_all_objects(Table),\\n                            [ets:insert(Table, E) || E <- ToKeep];\\n                        false ->\\n                            ok\\n                    end;\\n                _ ->\\n                    % Regular table - just clear if too large and not critical\\n                    case Table of\\n                        coding_agent_sessions -> ok;\\n                        coding_agent_crashes -> ok;\\n                        _ -> ets:delete_all_objects(Table)\\n                    end\\n            end;\\n        _ -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\ntrim_code() ->\\n    % Force full sweep GC and purge old code\\n    erlang:garbage_collect(),\\n    lists:foreach(fun(M) ->\\n        try\\n            code:soft_purge(M)\\n        catch\\n            _:_ -> ok  % Some modules can't be purged (system modules)\\n        end\\n    end, code:all_loaded()),\\n    ok.\\n\\ntrim_binary_heaps() ->\\n    %            undefined -> ok;\\n                _ -> \\n                    catch coding_agent_healer:report_crash(\\n                        coding_agent_process_monitor, \\n       undefined -> ok;\\n        Table ->\\n            try\\n                AllSessions = ets:tab2list(Table),\\n                Now = erlang:system_time(millisecond),\\n                OldThreshold                                  undefined -> ok;\\n                                        Pid when is_pid(Pid) -> catch gen_server:stop(Pid)\\n                                    end;\\n Sessions].\\n\\nclear_session_messages() ->\\n    Sessions = get_all_session_pids(),\\n    [catch flush_process_messages(Pid) || Pid <- Sessions].\\n\\nflush_process_messages(Pid) ->\\n    case ~p has ~p queued messages, killing~n\\\", [Pid, N]),\\n            exit(Pid, kill);\\n        _ ->\\n            ok\\n    end.\\n\\nget_all_session_pids() ->\\n    case ets:whereis(coding_agent_sessions) of\\n        undefined -> [];\\n        Table ->\\n            try\\n                [maps:get(pid, Data, undefined) || {_, Data} <- ets:tab2list(Table)]\\n            catch\\n                _:_ -> []\\n            end\\n    end.\\n\\ntrim_ets_tables() ->\\n    AllTables = ets:all(),\\n    [try trim_one_ets_table(T) catch _:_ -> ok end || T <- AllTables].\\n\\ntrim_one_ets_table(Table) ->\\n    case ets:info(Table, size) of\\n        N when N > 10000 ->\\n            io:format(\\\"[memory] ETS table ~p has ~p entries~n\\\", [Table, N]),\\n            % Keep most recent entries if possible\\n            case ets:info(Table, type) of\\n                ordered_set ->\\n                    % Ordered set - delete oldest\\n                    Sorted = ets:tab2list(Table),\\n                    case length(Sorted) > 1000 of\\n                        true ->\\n                            {ToKeep, _} = lists:split(1000, lists:reverse(Sorted)),\\n                            ets:delete_all_objects(Table),\\n                            [ets:insert(Table, E) || E <- ToKeep];\\n                        false ->\\n                            ok\\n                    end;\\n                _ ->\\n                    % Regular table - just clear if too large and not critical\\n                    case Table of\\n                        coding_agent_sessions -> ok;\\n                        coding_agent_crashes -> ok;\\n                        _ -> ets:delete_all_objects(Table)\\n                    end\\n            end;\\n        _ -> ok\\n    end.\\n\\ntrim_code() ->\\n    % Force full sweep GC and purge old code\\n    erlang:garbage_collect(),\\n    lists:foreach(fun(M) ->\\n        try\\n            code:soft_purge(M)\\n        catch\\n            _:_ -> ok  % Some modules can't be purged (system modules)\\n        end\\n    end, code:all_loaded()),\\n    ok.\\n\\ntrim_binary_heaps() ->\\n    % erlang:system_time(millisecond)),\\n    Pid = maps:get(pid, CrashInfo, unknown),\\n    Reason = maps:get(reason, CrashInfo, unknown),\\n    \\n    ReportContent = generate_process_crash_report(CrashId, CrashInfo),\\n    Filename = filename:join(?CRASH_DIR, binary_to_list(CrashId) ++ \\\".md\\\"),\\n    \\n    case file:write_file(Filename, ReportContent) of\\n        ok -> \\n            io:format(\\\"[memory] Crash report saved to ~s~n\\\", [Filename]);\\n        {error, Err} ->\\n            io:format(\\\"[memory] Failed to write crash report: ~p~n\\\", [Err])\\n    end.\\n\\ngenerate_process_crash_report(CrashId, CrashInfo) ->\\n    Timestamp = maps:get(timestamp, CrashInfo, 0),\\n    Pid = maps:get(pid, CrashInfo, unknown),\\n    Reason = maps:get(reason, CrashInfo, unknown),\\n    \\n    iolist_to_binary([\\n        <<\\\"# Process Crash Report\\\\n\\\\n\\\">>,\\n        io_lib:format(\\\"**Crash ID:** ~s\\\\n\\\\n\\\", [CrashId]),\\n
